<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" data-file-height="371" data-file-width="263" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Hangugeo-Chosonmal.svg/28px-Hangugeo-Chosonmal.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Hangugeo-Chosonmal.svg/42px-Hangugeo-Chosonmal.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Hangugeo-Chosonmal.svg/57px-Hangugeo-Chosonmal.svg.png 2x" width="28"/></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist" style="vertical-align:middle; font-size:95%;"><b>This article contains <a href="/wiki/Korean_language" title="Korean language">Korean</a> text.</b> Without proper <a href="/wiki/Help:Multilingual_support_(East_Asian)" title="Help:Multilingual support (East Asian)">rendering support</a>, you may see <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Replacement_character" title="Replacement character">question marks, boxes, or other symbols</a> instead of <a href="/wiki/Hangul" title="Hangul">Hangul</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hanja" title="Hanja">hanja</a>.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>South Korean girl group <a href="/wiki/Girls%27_Generation" title="Girls' Generation">Girls' Generation</a> has received various awards and nominations since their debut in 2007.</p>
<p>They rose to fame in 2009 with their hit single, "<a href="/wiki/Gee_(Girls%27_Generation_song)" title="Gee (Girls' Generation song)">Gee</a>", which later became known as "Song of the Decade".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> Within two days, the song became number one on all music charts and broke the record for longest-running number one on <i><a href="/wiki/Music_Bank_(TV_series)" title="Music Bank (TV series)">Music Bank</a></i> with nine consecutive wins.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> The group then released several hit singles such as "<a href="/wiki/Tell_Me_Your_Wish_(Genie)_(song)" title="Tell Me Your Wish (Genie) (song)">Tell Me Your Wish (Genie)</a>" in 2009, "<a href="/wiki/Oh!_(Girls%27_Generation_song)" title="Oh! (Girls' Generation song)">Oh!</a>" in 2010, "<a href="/wiki/The_Boys_(Girls%27_Generation_song)" title="The Boys (Girls' Generation song)">The Boys</a>" in 2011, "<a href="/wiki/I_Got_a_Boy_(song)" title="I Got a Boy (song)">I Got a Boy</a>" in 2013 and "<a href="/wiki/Lion_Heart_(song)" title="Lion Heart (song)">Lion Heart</a>" in 2015. The group became the first girl group to win both a Disk Daesang (2010) and a Digital Daesang (2009) at the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Disc_Awards" title="Golden Disc Awards">Golden Disc Awards</a>, and also the first girl group to win Daesang award three times in a row.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_programs">Music programs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Girls%27_Generation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Music programs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Inkigayo"><i>Inkigayo</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Girls%27_Generation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Inkigayo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Inkigayo" title="Inkigayo">Inkigayo</a></i> (인기가요; <i>The Music Trend</i>) is a music television program aired by <a href="/wiki/Seoul_Broadcasting_System" title="Seoul Broadcasting System">Seoul Broadcasting System</a> (SBS). As of 2015, Girls' Generation has won 27 times.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="M_Countdown"><i>M Countdown</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Girls%27_Generation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: M Countdown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/M_Countdown" title="M Countdown">M Countdown</a></i> is a South Korean music program broadcast by <a href="/wiki/Mnet_(TV_channel)" title="Mnet (TV channel)">Mnet</a>. Girls' Generation has won 18 times as of 2015, including three songs achieving Triple Crown awards, "The Boys", "I Got a Boy" and "Lion Heart".</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_Bank"><i>Music Bank</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Girls%27_Generation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Music Bank">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Music_Bank_(TV_series)" title="Music Bank (TV series)">Music Bank</a></i> is a South Korean music television program broadcast by <a href="/wiki/Korean_Broadcasting_System" title="Korean Broadcasting System">Korean Broadcasting System</a> (KBS). As of 2015, Girls' Generation has received 42 wins on <i>Music Bank</i>. In 2009, the group's single "Gee" claimed the number-one spot for a record-breaking nine consecutive weeks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Show"><i>The Show</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Girls%27_Generation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: The Show">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/The_Show_(South_Korean_TV_series)" title="The Show (South Korean TV series)">The Show</a></i> (더 쇼) is a South Korean music program aired by <a href="/wiki/SBS_MTV" title="SBS MTV">SBS MTV</a>. Girls' Generation has won two times as of 2015 with "Party" and "Lion Heart".</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Show_Champion"><i>Show Champion</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Girls%27_Generation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Show Champion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Show_Champion" title="Show Champion">Show Champion</a></i> is a South Korean music program aired by <a href="/wiki/MBC_Music" title="MBC Music">MBC Music</a>. Girls' Generation has won four times as of 2015.</p>
<table class="wikitable" style="table-layout: fixed; margin-right:0; text-align:center">
<tr>
<th width="5%">Year</th>
<th width="45%">Date</th>
<th width="50%">Song</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="2">2014</td>
<td>March 12</td>
<td rowspan="2">"Mr.Mr."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>March 19</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="2">2015</td>
<td>July 15</td>
<td>"Party"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>August 26</td>
<td>"Lion Heart"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup></td>
</tr>
</table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Show.21_Music_Core"><i>Show! Music Core</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Girls%27_Generation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Show! Music Core">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Show!_Music_Core" title="Show! Music Core">Show! Music Core</a></i>, broadcast by <a href="/wiki/Munhwa_Broadcasting_Corporation" title="Munhwa Broadcasting Corporation">Munhwa Broadcasting Corporation</a> (MBC), is a South Korean music program. As of 2015, Girls' Generation achieved five wins on <i>Show! Music Core</i> with "Mr.Mr.", "Party " and "Lion Heart".</p>
<table class="wikitable" style="table-layout: fixed; margin-right:0; text-align:center">
<tr>
<th width="5%">Year</th>

</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="2">2014</td>
<td>March 15</td>
<td rowspan="2">"Mr.Mr."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>March 22</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="3">2015</td>
<td>July 18</td>
<td>"Party"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>August 29</td>
<td rowspan="2">"Lion Heart"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup></td>

</tr>

<p><b>Note:</b> Music Core brought back the show's chart on April 20, 2013.</p>
